<s> THE LAST GALLEY IMPRESSIONS AND TALES By Arthur Conan Doyle PREFACE I have written "Impressions and Tales" upon the title-page of this volume, because I have included within the same cover two styles of work which present an essential difference </s>
<s> The second half of the collection consists of eight stories, which explain themselves </s>
<s> The first half is made up of a series of pictures of the past which maybe regarded as trial flights towards a larger ideal which I have long had in my mind </s>
<s> It has seemed to me that there is a region between actual story and actual history which has never been adequately exploited </s>
<s> I could imagine, for example, a work dealing with some great historical epoch, and finding its interest not in the happenings to particular individuals, their adventures and their loves, but in the fascination of the actual facts of history themselves </s>
<s> These facts might be coloured with the glamour which the writer of fiction can give, and fictitious characters and conversations might illustrate them; but none the less the actual drama of history and not the drama of invention should claim the attention of the reader </s>
<s> I have been tempted sometimes to try the effect upon a larger scale; but meanwhile these short sketches, portraying various crises in the story of the human race, are to be judged as experiments in that direction </s>
<s> ARTHUR CONAN DOYLE </s>
<s> WINDLESHAM, CROWBOROUGH, April, 1911 </s>
<s> CONTENTS PART I THE LAST GALLEY THE CONTEST THROUGH THE VEIL AN ICONOCLAST GIANT MAXIMIN THE COMING OF THE HUNS THE LAST OF THE LEGIONS THE FIRST CARGO THE HOME-COMING THE RED STAR PART II THE SILVER MIRROR THE BLIGHTING OF SHARKEY THE MARRIAGE OF THE BRIGADIER THE LORD OF FALCONBRIDGE OUT OF THE RUNNING "DE PROFUNDIS" THE GREAT BROWN-PERICORD MOTOR THE TERROR OF BLUE JOHN GAP PART I </s>
<s> THE LAST GALLEY "Mutato nomine, de te, Britannia, fabula narratur" </s>
<s> It was a spring morning, one hundred and forty-six years before the coming of Christ </s>
<s> The North African Coast, with its broad hem of golden sand, its green belt of feathery palm trees, and its background of barren, red-scarped hills, shimmered like a dream country in the opal light </s>
<s> Save for a narrow edge of snow-white surf, the Mediterranean lay blue and serene as far as the eye could reach </s>
<s> In all its vast expanse there was no break but for a single galley, which was slowly making its way from the direction of Sicily and heading for the distant harbour of Carthage </s>
<s> Seen from afar it was a stately and beautiful vessel, deep red in colour, double-banked with scarlet oars, its broad, flapping sail stained with Tyrian purple, its bulwarks gleaming with brass work </s>
<s> A brazen, three-pronged ram projected in front, and a high golden figure of Baal, the God of the Phoenicians, children of Canaan, shone upon the after deck </s>
<s> From the single high mast above the huge sail streamed the tiger-striped flag of Carthage </s>
<s> So, like some stately scarlet bird, with golden beak and wings of purple, she swam upon the face of the waters--a thing of might and of beauty as seen from the distant shore </s>
<s> But approach and look at her now </s>
<s> What are these dark streaks which foul her white decks and dapple her brazen shields </s>
<s> Why do the long red oars move out of time, irregular, convulsive </s>
<s> Why are some missing from the staring portholes, some snapped with jagged, yellow edges, some trailing inert against the side </s>
<s> Why are two prongs of the brazen ram twisted and broken </s>
<s> See, even the high image of Baal is battered and disfigured </s>
<s> By every sign this ship has passed through some grievous trial, some day of terror, which has left its heavy marks upon her </s>
<s> And now stand upon the deck itself, and see more closely the men who man her </s>
<s> There are two decks forward and aft, while in the open waist are the double banks of seats, above and below, where the rowers, two to an oar, tug and bend at their endless task </s>
<s> Down the centre is a narrow platform, along which pace a line of warders, lash in hand, who cut cruelly at the slave who pauses, be it only for an instant, to sweep the sweat from his dripping brow </s>
<s> But these slaves--look at them </s>
<s> Some are captured Romans, some Sicilians, many black Libyans, but all are in the last exhaustion, their weary eyelids drooped over their eyes, their lips thick with black crusts, and pink with bloody froth, their arms and backs moving mechanically to the hoarse chant of the overseer </s>
<s> Their bodies of all tints from ivory to jet, are stripped to the waist, and every glistening back shows the angry stripes of the warders </s>
<s> But it is not from these that the blood comes which reddens the seats and tints the salt water washing beneath their manacled feet </s>
<s> Great gaping wounds, the marks of sword slash and spear stab, show crimson upon their naked chests and shoulders, while many lie huddled and senseless athwart the benches, careless for ever of the whips which still hiss above them </s>
<s> Now we can understand those empty portholes and those trailing oars </s>
<s> Nor were the crew in better case than their slaves </s>
<s> The decks were littered with wounded and dying men </s>
<s> It was but a remnant who still remained upon their feet </s>
<s> The most lay exhausted upon the fore-deck, while a few of the more zealous were mending their shattered armour, restringing their bows, or cleaning the deck from the marks of combat </s>
<s> Upon a raised platform at the base of the mast stood the sailing-master who conned the ship, his eyes fixed upon the distant point of Megara which screened the eastern side of the Bay of Carthage </s>
<s> On the after-deck were gathered a number of officers, silent and brooding, glancing from time to time at two of their own class who stood apart deep in conversation </s>
<s> The one, tall, dark, and wiry, with pure, Semitic features, and the limbs of a giant, was Magro, the famous Carthaginian captain, whose name was still a terror on every shore, from Gaul to the Euxine </s>
<s> The other, a white-bearded, swarthy man, with indomitable courage and energy stamped upon every eager line of his keen, aquiline face, was Gisco the politician, a man of the highest Punic blood, a Suffete of the purple robe, and the leader of that party in the State which had watched and striven amid the selfishness and slothfulness of his fellow-countrymen to rouse the public spirit and waken the public conscience to the ever-increasing danger from Rome </s>
<s> As they talked, the two men glanced continually, with earnest anxious faces, towards the northern skyline </s>
<s> "It is certain," said the older man, with gloom in his voice and bearing, "none have escaped save ourselves" </s>
<s> "I did not leave the press of the battle whilst I saw one ship which I could succour," Magro answered </s>
<s> "As it was, we came away, as you saw, like a wolf which has a hound hanging on to either haunch </s>
<s> The Roman dogs can show the wolf-bites which prove it </s>
<s> Had any other galley won clear, they would surely be with us by now, since they have no place of safety save Carthage" </s>
<s> The younger warrior glanced keenly ahead to the distant point which marked his native city </s>
<s> Already the low, leafy hill could be seen, dotted with the white villas of the wealthy Phoenician merchants </s>
<s> Above them, a gleaming dot against the pale blue morning sky, shone the brazen roof of the citadel of Byrsa, which capped the sloping town </s>
<s> "Already they can see us from the watch-towers," he remarked </s>
<s> "Even from afar they may know the galley of Black Magro </s>
<s> But which of all of them will guess that we alone remain of all that goodly fleet which sailed out with blare of trumpet and roll of drum but one short month ago" </s>
<s> The patrician smiled bitterly </s>
<s> "If it were not for our great ancestors and for our beloved country, the Queen of the Waters," said he, "I could find it in my heart to be glad at this destruction which has come upon this vain and feeble generation </s>
<s> You have spent your life upon the seas, Magro </s>
<s> You do not know of know how it has been with us on the land </s>
<s> But I have seen this canker grow upon us which now leads us to our death </s>
<s> I and others have gone down into the market-place to plead with the people, and been pelted with mud for our pains </s>
<s> Many a time have I pointed to Rome, and said, 'Behold these people, who bear arms themselves, each man for his own duty and pride </s>
<s> How can you who hide behind mercenaries hope to stand against them'?--a hundred times I have said it" </s>
<s> "And had they no answer" </s>
<s> asked the Rover </s>
<s> "Rome was far off and they could not see it, so to them it was nothing," the old man answered </s>
<s> "Some thought of trade, and some of votes, and some of profits from the State, but none would see that the State itself, the mother of all things, was sinking to her end </s>
<s> So might the bees debate who should have wax or honey when the torch was blazing which would bring to ashes the hive and all therein </s>
<s> 'Are we not rulers of the sea' </s>
<s> 'Was not Hannibal a great man' </s>
<s> Such were their cries, living ever in the past and blind to the future </s>
<s> Before that sun sets there will be tearing of hair and rending of garments; what will that now avail us" </s>
<s> "It is some sad comfort," said Magro, "to know that what Rome holds she cannot keep" </s>
<s> "Why say you that </s>
<s> When we go down, she is supreme in all the world" </s>
<s> "For a time, and only for a time," Magro answered, gravely </s>
<s> "Yet you will smile, perchance, when I tell you how it is that I know it </s>
<s> There was a wise woman who lived in that part of the Tin Islands which juts forth into the sea, and from her lips I have heard many things, but not one which has not come aright </s>
<s> Of the fall of our own country, and even of this battle, from which we now return, she told me clearly </s>
<s> There is much strange lore amongst these savage peoples in the west of the land of Tin" </s>
<s> "What said she of Rome" </s>
<s> "That she also would fall, even as we, weakened by her riches and her factions" </s>
<s> Gisco rubbed his hands </s>
<s> "That at least makes our own fall less bitter," said he </s>
<s> "But since we have fallen, and Rome will fall, who in turn may hope to be Queen of the Waters" </s>
<s> "That also I asked her," said Magro, "and gave her my Tyrian belt with the golden buckle as a guerdon for her answer </s>
<s> But, indeed, it was too high payment for the tale she told, which must be false if all else she said was true </s>
<s> She would have it that in coining days it was her own land, this fog-girt isle where painted savages can scarce row a wicker coracle from point to point, which shall at last take the trident which Carthage and Rome have dropped" </s>
<s> The smile which flickered upon the old patrician's keen features died away suddenly, and his fingers closed upon his companion's wrist </s>
<s> The other had set rigid, his head advanced, his hawk eyes upon the northern skyline </s>
<s> Its straight, blue horizon was broken by two low black dots </s>
<s> "Galleys" </s>
<s> whispered Gisco </s>
<s> The whole crew had seen them </s>
<s> They clustered along the starboard bulwarks, pointing and chattering </s>
<s> For a moment the gloom of defeat was lifted, and a buzz of joy ran from group to group at the thought that they were not alone--that some one had escaped the great carnage as well as themselves </s>
<s> "By the spirit of Baal," said Black Magro, "I could not have believed that any could have fought clear from such a welter </s>
<s> Could it be young Hamilcar in the _Africa_, or is it Beneva in the blue Syrian ship </s>
<s> We three with others may form a squadron and make head against them yet </s>
<s> If we hold our course, they will join us ere we round the harbour mole" </s>
<s> Slowly the injured galley toiled on her way, and more swiftly the two newcomers swept down from the north </s>
<s> Only a few miles off lay the green point and the white houses which flanked the great African city </s>
<s> Already, upon the headland, could be seen a dark group of waiting townsmen </s>
<s> Gisco and Magro were still watching with puckered gaze the approaching galleys, when the brown Libyan boatswain, with flashing teeth and gleaming eyes, rushed upon the poop, his long thin arm stabbing to the north </s>
<s> "Romans" </s>
<s> he cried </s>
<s> "Romans" </s>
<s> A hush had fallen over the great vessel </s>
<s> Only the wash of the water and the measured rattle and beat of the oars broke in upon the silence </s>
<s> "By the horns of God's altar, I believe the fellow is right" </s>
<s> cried old Gisco </s>
<s> "See how they swoop upon us like falcons </s>
<s> They are full-manned and full-oared" </s>
<s> "Plain wood, unpainted," said Magro </s>
<s> "See how it gleams yellow where the sun strikes it" </s>
<s> "And yonder thing beneath the mast </s>
<s> Is it not the cursed bridge they use for boarding" </s>
<s> "So they grudge us even one," said Magro with a bitter laugh </s>
<s> "Not even one galley shall return to the old sea-mother </s>
<s> Well, for my part, I would as soon have it so </s>
<s> I am of a mind to stop the oars and await them" </s>
<s> "It is a man's thought," answered old Gisco; "but the city will need us in the days to come </s>
<s> What shall it profit us to make the Roman victory complete </s>
<s> Nay, Magro, let the slaves row as they never rowed before, not for our own safety, but for the profit of the State" </s>
<s> So the great red ship laboured and lurched onwards, like a weary panting stag which seeks shelter from his pursuers, while ever swifter and ever nearer sped the two lean fierce galleys from the north </s>
<s> Already the morning sun shone upon the lines of low Roman helmets above the bulwarks, and glistened on the silver wave where each sharp prow shot through the still blue water </s>
<s> Every moment the ships drew nearer, and the long thin scream of the Roman trumpets grew louder upon the ear </s>
<s> Upon the high bluff of Megara there stood a great concourse of the people of Carthage who had hurried forth from the city upon the news that the galleys were in sight </s>
<s> They stood now, rich and poor, effete and plebeian, white Phoenician and dark Kabyle, gazing with breathless interest at the spectacle before them </s>
<s> Some hundreds of feet beneath them the Punic galley had drawn so close that with their naked eyes they could see those stains of battle which told their dismal tale </s>
<s> The Romans, too, were heading in such a way that it was before their very faces that their ship was about to be cut off; and yet of all this multitude not one could raise a hand in its defence </s>
<s> Some wept in impotent grief, some cursed with flashing eyes and knotted fists, some on their knees held up appealing hands to Baal; but neither prayer, tears, nor curses could undo the past nor mend the present </s>
<s> That broken, crawling galley meant that their fleet was gone </s>
<s> Those two fierce darting ships meant that the hands of Rome were already at their throat </s>
<s> Behind them would come others and others, the innumerable trained hosts of the great Republic, long mistress of the land, now dominant also upon the waters </s>
<s> In a month, two months, three at the most, their armies would be there, and what could all the untrained multitudes of Carthage do to stop them </s>
<s> "Nay" </s>
<s> cried one, more hopeful than the rest, "at least we are brave men with arms in our hands" </s>
<s> "Fool" </s>
<s> said another, "is it not such talk which has brought us to our ruin </s>
<s> What is the brave man untrained to the brave man trained </s>
<s> When you stand before the sweep and rush of a Roman legion you may learn the difference" </s>
<s> "Then let us train" </s>
<s> "Too late </s>
<s> A full year is needful to turn a man to a soldier </s>
<s> Where will you--where will your city be within the year </s>
<s> Nay, there is but one chance for us </s>
<s> If we give up our commerce and our colonies, if we strip ourselves of all that made us great, then perchance the Roman conqueror may hold his hand" </s>
<s> And already the last sea-fight of Carthage was coming swiftly to an end before them </s>
<s> Under their very eyes the two Roman galleys had shot in, one on either side of the vessel of Black Magro </s>
<s> They had grappled with him, and he, desperate in his despair, had cast the crooked flukes of his anchors over their gunwales, and bound them to him in an iron grip, whilst with hammer and crowbar he burst great holes in his own sheathing </s>
<s> The last Punic galley should never be rowed into Ostia, a sight for the holiday-makers of Rome </s>
<s> She would lie in her own waters </s>
<s> And the fierce, dark soul of her rover captain glowed as he thought that not alone should she sink into the depths of the mother sea </s>
<s> Too late did the Romans understand the man with whom they had to deal </s>
<s> Their boarders who had flooded the Punic decks felt the planking sink and sway beneath them </s>
<s> They rushed to gain their own vessels; but they, too, were being drawn downwards, held in the dying grip of the great red galley </s>
<s> Over they went and ever over </s>
<s> Now the deck of Magro's ship is flush with the water, and the Romans, drawn towards it by the iron bonds which held them, are tilted downwards, one bulwark upon the waves, one reared high in the air </s>
<s> Madly they strain to cast off the death grip of the galley </s>
<s> She is under the surface now, and ever swifter, with the greater weight, the Roman ships heel after her </s>
<s> There is a rending crash </s>
<s> The wooden side is torn out of one, and mutilated, dismembered, she rights herself, and lies a helpless thing upon the water </s>
<s> But a last yellow gleam in the blue water shows where her consort has been dragged to her end in the iron death-grapple of her foemen </s>
<s> The tiger-striped flag of Carthage has sunk beneath the swirling surface, never more to be seen upon the face of the sea </s>
<s> For in that year a great cloud hung for seventeen days over the African coast, a deep black cloud which was the dark shroud of the burning city </s>
<s> And when the seventeen days were over, Roman ploughs were driven from end to end of the charred ashes, and salt was scattered there as a sign that Carthage should be no more </s>
<s> And far off a huddle of naked, starving folk stood upon the distant mountains, and looked down upon the desolate plain which had once been the fairest and richest upon earth </s>
<s> And they understood too late that it is the law of heaven that the world is given to the hardy and to the self-denying, whilst he who would escape the duties of manhood will soon be stripped of the pride, the wealth, and the power, which are the prizes which manhood brings </s>
<s> THE CONTEST </s>
<s> In the year of our Lord 66, the Emperor Nero, being at that time in the twenty-ninth year of his life and the thirteenth of his reign, set sail for Greece with the strangest company and the most singular design that any monarch has ever entertained </s>
<s> With ten galleys he went forth from Puteoli, carrying with him great stores of painted scenery and theatrical properties, together with a number of knights and senators, whom he feared to leave behind him at Rome, and who were all marked for death in the course of his wanderings </s>
<s> In his train he took Natus, his singing coach; Cluvius, a man with a monstrous voice, who should bawl out his titles; and a thousand trained youths who had learned to applaud in unison whenever their master sang or played in public </s>
<s> So deftly had they been taught that each had his own role to play </s>
<s> Some did no more than give forth a low deep hum of speechless appreciation </s>
<s> Some clapped with enthusiasm </s>
<s> Some, rising from approbation into absolute frenzy, shrieked, stamped, and beat sticks upon the benches </s>
<s> Some--and they were the most effective--had learned from an Alexandrian a long droning musical note which they all uttered together, so that it boomed over the assembly </s>
<s> With the aid of these mercenary admirers, Nero had every hope, in spite of his indifferent voice and clumsy execution, to return to Rome, bearing with him the chaplets for song offered for free competition by the Greek cities </s>
<s> As his great gilded galley with two tiers of oars passed down the Mediterranean, the Emperor sat in his cabin all day, his teacher by his side, rehearsing from morning to night those compositions which he had selected, whilst every few hours a Nubian slave massaged the Imperial throat with oil and balsam, that it might be ready for the great ordeal which lay before it in the land of poetry and song </s>
<s> His food, his drink, and his exercise were prescribed for him as for an athlete who trains for a contest, and the twanging of his lyre, with the strident notes of his voice, resounded continually from the Imperial quarters </s>
<s> Now it chanced that there lived in those days a Grecian goatherd named Policles, who tended and partly owned a great flock which grazed upon the long flanks of the hills near Heroea, which is five miles north of the river Alpheus, and no great distance from the famous Olympia </s>
<s> This person was noted all over the countryside as a man of strange gifts and singular character </s>
<s> He was a poet who had twice been crowned for his verses, and he was a musician to whom the use and sound of an instrument were so natural that one would more easily meet him without his staff than his harp </s>
<s> Even in his lonely vigils on the winter hills he would bear it always slung over his shoulder, and would pass the long hours by its aid, so that it had come to be part of his very self </s>
<s> He was beautiful also, swarthy and eager, with a head like Adonis, and in strength there was no one who could compete with him </s>
<s> But all was ruined by his disposition, which was so masterful that he would brook no opposition nor contradiction </s>
<s> For this reason he was continually at enmity with all his neighbours, and in his fits of temper he would spend months at a time in his stone hut among the mountains, hearing nothing from the world, and living only for his music and his goats </s>
<s> One spring morning, in the year of 67, Policles, with the aid of his boy Dorus, had driven his goats over to a new pasturage which overlooked from afar the town of Olympia </s>
<s> Gazing down upon it from the mountain, the shepherd was surprised to see that a portion of the famous amphitheatre had been roofed in, as though some performance was being enacted </s>
<s> Living far from the world and from all news, Policles could not imagine what was afoot, for he was well aware that the Grecian games were not due for two years to come </s>
<s> Surely some poetic or musical contest must be proceeding of which he had heard nothing </s>
<s> If so, there would perhaps be some chance of his gaining the votes of the judges; and in any case he loved to hear the compositions and admire the execution of the great minstrels who assembled on such an occasion </s>
<s> Calling to Dorus, therefore, he left the goats to his charge, and strode swiftly away, his harp upon his back, to see what was going forward in the town </s>
<s> When Policles came into the suburbs, he found them deserted; but he was still more surprised when he reached the main street to see no single human being in the place </s>
<s> He hastened his steps, therefore, and as he approached the theatre he was conscious of a low sustained hum which announced the concourse of a huge assembly </s>
<s> Never in all his dreams had he imagined any musical competition upon so vast a scale as this </s>
<s> There were some soldiers clustering outside the door; but Policles pushed his way swiftly through them, and found himself upon the outskirts of the multitude who filled the great space formed by roofing over a portion of the national stadium </s>
<s> Looking around him, Policles saw a great number of his neighbours, whom he knew by sight, tightly packed upon the benches, all with their eyes fixed upon the stage </s>
<s> He also observed that there were soldiers round the walls, and that a considerable part of the hall was filled by a body of youths of foreign aspect, with white gowns and long hair </s>
<s> All this he perceived; but what it meant he could not imagine </s>
<s> He bent over to a neighbour to ask him, but a soldier prodded him at once with the butt end of his spear, and commanded him fiercely to hold his peace </s>
<s> The man whom he had addressed, thinking that Policles had demanded a seat, pressed closer to his neighbour, and so the shepherd found himself sitting at the end of the bench which was nearest to the door </s>
<s> Thence he concentrated himself upon the stage, on which Metas, a well-known minstrel from Corinth and an old friend of Policles, was singing and playing without much encouragement from the audience </s>
<s> To Policles it seemed that Metas was having less than his due, so he applauded loudly, but he was surprised to observe that the soldiers frowned at him, and that all his neighbours regarded him with some surprise </s>
<s> Being a man of strong and obstinate character, he was the more inclined to persevere in his clapping when he perceived that the general sentiment was against him </s>
<s> But what followed filled the shepherd poet with absolute amazement </s>
<s> When Metas of Corinth had made his bow and withdrawn to half-hearted and perfunctory applause, there appeared upon the stage, amid the wildest enthusiasm upon the part of the audience, a most extraordinary figure </s>
<s> He was a short fat man, neither old nor young, with a bull neck and a round, heavy face, which hung in creases in front like the dewlap of an ox </s>
<s> He was absurdly clad in a short blue tunic, braced at the waist with a golden belt </s>
<s> His neck and part of his chest were exposed, and his short, fat legs were bare from the buskins below to the middle of his thighs, which was as far as his tunic extended </s>
<s> In his hair were two golden wings, and the same upon his heels, after the fashion of the god Mercury </s>
<s> Behind him walked a negro bearing a harp, and beside him a richly dressed officer who bore rolls of music </s>
<s> This strange creature took the harp from the hands of the attendant, and advanced to the front of the stage, whence he bowed and smiled to the cheering audience </s>
<s> "This is some foppish singer from Athens," thought Policles to himself, but at the same time he understood that only a great master of song could receive such a reception from a Greek audience </s>
<s> This was evidently some wonderful performer whose reputation had preceded him </s>
<s> Policles settled down, therefore, and prepared to give his soul up to the music </s>
<s> The blue-clad player struck several chords upon his lyre, and then burst suddenly out into the "Ode of Niobe" </s>
<s> Policles sat straight up on his bench and gazed at the stage in amazement </s>
<s> The tune demanded a rapid transition from a low note to a high, and had been purposely chosen for this reason </s>
<s> The low note was a grunting, a rumble, the deep discordant growling of an ill-conditioned dog </s>
<s> Then suddenly the singer threw up his face, straightened his tubby figure, rose upon his tiptoes, and with wagging head and scarlet cheeks emitted such a howl as the same dog might have given had his growl been checked by a kick from his master </s>
<s> All the while the lyre twanged and thrummed, sometimes in front of and sometimes behind the voice of the singer </s>
<s> But what amazed Policles most of all was the effect of this performance upon the audience </s>
<s> Every Greek was a trained critic, and as unsparing in his hisses as he was lavish in his applause </s>
<s> Many a singer far better than this absurd fop had been driven amid execration and abuse from the platform </s>
<s> But now, as the man stopped and wiped the abundant sweat from his fat face, the whole assembly burst into a delirium of appreciation </s>
<s> The shepherd held his hands to his bursting head, and felt that his reason must be leaving him </s>
<s> It was surely a dreadful musical nightmare, and he would wake soon and laugh at the remembrance </s>
<s> But no; the figures were real, the faces were those of his neighbours, the cheers which resounded in his ears were indeed from an audience which filled the theatre of Olympia </s>
<s> The whole chorus was in full blast, the hummers humming, the shouters bellowing, the tappers hard at work upon the benches, while every now and then came a musical cyclone of "Incomparable </s>
<s> Divine" </s>
<s> from the trained phalanx who intoned their applause, their united voices sweeping over the tumult as the drone of the wind dominates the roar of the sea </s>
<s> It was madness--insufferable madness </s>
<s> If this were allowed to pass, there was an end of all musical justice in Greece </s>
<s> Policles' conscience would not permit him to be still </s>
<s> Standing upon his bench with waving hands and upraised voice, he protested with all the strength of his lungs against the mad judgment of the audience </s>
<s> At first, amid the tumult, his action was hardly noticed </s>

<s> AN ICONOCLAST </s>
<s> It was daybreak of a March morning in the year of Christ 92 </s>
<s> Outside the long Semita Alta was already thronged with people, with buyers and sellers, callers and strollers, for the Romans were so early-rising a people that many a Patrician preferred to see his clients at six in the morning </s>
<s> Such was the good republican tradition, still upheld by the more conservative; but with more modern habits of luxury, a night of pleasure and banqueting was no uncommon thing </s>

<s> GIANT MAXIMIN </s>
<s> I THE COMING OF MAXIMIN Many are the strange vicissitudes of history </s>
<s> Greatness has often sunk to the dust, and has tempered itself to its new surrounding </s>
<s> Smallness has risen aloft, has flourished for a time, and then has sunk once more </s>
<s> Rich monarchs have become poor monks, brave conquerors have lost their manhood, eunuchs and women have overthrown armies and kingdoms </s>
<s> Surely there is no situation which the mind of man can invent which has not taken shape and been played out upon the world stage </s>
<s> But of all the strange careers and of all the wondrous happenings, stranger than Charles in his monastery, or Justin on his throne, there stands the case of Giant Maximin, what he attained, and how he attained it </s>
<s> Let me tell the sober facts of history, tinged only by that colouring to which the more austere historians could not condescend </s>
<s> It is a record as well as a story </s>
<s> In the heart of Thrace some ten miles north of the Rhodope mountains, there is a valley which is named Harpessus, after the stream which runs down it </s>
<s> Through this valley lies the main road from the east to the west, and along the road, returning from an expedition against the Alani, there marched, upon the fifth day of the month of June in the year 210, a small but compact Roman army </s>
<s> It consisted of three legions--the Jovian, the Cappadocian, and the men of Hercules </s>
<s> Ten turmae of Gallic cavalry led the van, whilst the rear was covered by a regiment of Batavian Horse Guards, the immediate attendants of the Emperor Septimus Severus who had conducted the campaign in person </s>
<s> The peasants who lined the low hills which fringed the valley looked with indifference upon the long files of dusty, heavily-burdened infantry, but they broke into murmurs of delight at the gold-faced cuirasses and high brazen horse-hair helmets of the guardsmen, applauding their stalwart figures, their martial bearing, and the stately black chargers which they rode </s>
<s> A soldier might know that it was the little weary men with their short swords, their heavy pikes over their shoulders, and their square shields slung upon their backs, who were the real terror of the enemies of the Empire, but to the eyes of the wondering Thracians it was this troop of glittering Apollos who bore Rome's victory upon their banners, and upheld the throne of the purple-togaed prince who rode before them </s>
<s> Among the scattered groups of peasants who looked on from a respectful distance at this military pageant, there were two men who attracted much attention from those who stood immediately around them </s>
<s> The one was commonplace enough--a little grey-headed man, with uncouth dress and a frame which was bent and warped by a long life of arduous toil, goat-driving and wood-chopping among the mountains </s>
<s> It was the appearance of his youthful companion which had drawn the amazed observation of the bystanders </s>
<s> In stature he was such a giant as is seen but once or twice in each generation of mankind </s>
<s> Eight feet and two inches was his measure from his sandalled sole to the topmost curls of his tangled hair </s>
<s> Yet for all his mighty stature there was nothing heavy or clumsy in the man </s>
<s> His huge shoulders bore no redundant flesh, and his figure was straight and hard and supple as a young pine tree </s>
<s> A frayed suit of brown leather clung close to his giant body, and a cloak of undressed sheep-skin was slung from his shoulder </s>
<s> His bold blue eyes, shock of yellow hair and fair skin showed that he was of Gothic or northern blood, and the amazed expression upon his broad frank face as he stared at the passing troops told of a simple and uneventful life in some back valley of the Macedonian mountains </s>
<s> "I fear your mother was right when she advised that we keep you at home," said the old man anxiously </s>
<s> "Tree-cutting and wood-carrying will seem but dull work after such a sight as this" </s>
<s> "When I see mother next it will be to put a golden torque round her neck," said the young giant </s>
<s> "And you, daddy; I will fill your leather pouch with gold pieces before I have done" </s>
<s> The old man looked at his son with startled eyes </s>
<s> "You would not leave us, Theckla </s>
<s> What could we do without you" </s>
<s> "My place is down among yonder men," said the young man </s>
<s> "I was not born to drive goats and carry logs, but to sell this manhood of mine in the best market </s>
<s> There is my market in the Emperor's own Guard </s>
<s> Say nothing, daddy, for my mind is set, and if you weep now it will be to laugh hereafter </s>
<s> I will to great Rome with the soldiers" </s>
<s> The daily march of the heavily laden Roman legionary was fixed at twenty miles; but on this afternoon, though only half the distance had been accomplished, the silver trumpets blared out their welcome news that a camp was to be formed </s>
<s> As the men broke their ranks, the reason of their light march was announced by the decurions </s>
<s> It was the birthday of Geta, the younger son of the Emperor, and in his honour there would be games and a double ration of wine </s>
<s> But the iron discipline of the Roman army required that under all circumstances certain duties should be performed, and foremost among them that the camp should be made secure </s>
<s> Laying down their arms in the order of their ranks, the soldiers seized their spades and axes, and worked rapidly and joyously until sloping vallum and gaping fossa girdled them round, and gave them safe refuge against a night attack </s>
<s> Then in noisy, laughing, gesticulating crowds they gathered in their thousands round the grassy arena where the sports were to be held </s>
<s> A long green hillside sloped down to a level plain, and on this gentle incline the army lay watching the strife of the chosen athletes who contended before them </s>
<s> They stretched themselves in the glare of the sunshine, their heavy tunics thrown off, and their naked limbs sprawling, wine-cups an baskets of fruit and cakes circling amongst them, enjoying rest and peace as only those can to whom it comes so rarely </s>
<s> The five-mile race was over, and had been won as usual by Decurion Brennus, the crack long-distance champion of the Herculians </s>
<s> Amid the yells of the Jovians, Capellus of the corps had carried off both the long and the high jump </s>
<s> Big Brebix the Gaul had out-thrown the long guardsman Serenus with the fifty pound stone </s>
<s> Now, as the sun sank towards the western ridge, and turned the Harpessus to a riband of gold, they had come to the final of the wrestling, where the pliant Greek, whose name is lost in the nickname of "Python," was tried out against the bull-necked Lictor of the military police, a hairy Hercules, whose heavy hand had in the way of duty oppressed many of the spectators </s>
<s> As the two men, stripped save for their loin-cloths, approached the wrestling-ring, cheers and counter-cheers burst from their adherents, some favouring the Lictor for his Roman blood, some the Greek from their own private grudge </s>
<s> And then, of a sudden, the cheering died, heads were turned towards the slope away from the arena, men stood up and peered and pointed, until finally, in a strange hush, the whole great assembly had forgotten the athletes, and were watching a single man walking swiftly towards them down the green curve of the hill </s>
<s> This huge solitary figure, with the oaken club in his hand, the shaggy fleece flapping from his great shoulders, and the setting sun gleaming upon a halo of golden hair, might have been the tutelary god of the fierce and barren mountains from which he had issued </s>
<s> Even the Emperor rose from his chair and gazed with open-eyed amazement at the extraordinary being who approached him </s>
<s> The man, whom we already know as Theckla the Thracian, paid no heed to the attention which he had aroused, but strode onwards, stepping as lightly as a deer, until he reached the fringe of the soldiers </s>
<s> Amid their open ranks he picked his way, sprang over the ropes which guarded the arena, and advanced towards the Emperor, until a spear at his breast warned him that he must go no nearer </s>
<s> Then he sunk upon his right knee and called out some words in the Gothic speech </s>
<s> "Great Jupiter </s>
<s> Whoever saw such a body of a man" </s>
<s> cried the Emperor </s>
<s> "What says he </s>
<s> What is amiss with the fellow </s>
<s> Whence comes he, and what is his name" </s>
<s> An interpreter translated the Barbarian's answer </s>
<s> "He says, great Caesar, that he is of good blood, and sprung by a Gothic father from a woman of the Alani </s>
<s> He says that his name is Theckla, and that he would fain carry a sword in Caesar's service" </s>
<s> The Emperor smiled </s>
<s> "Some post could surely be found for such a man, were it but as janitor at the Palatine Palace," said he to one of the Prefects </s>
<s> "I would fain see him walk even as he is through the forum </s>
<s> He would turn the heads of half the women in Rome </s>
<s> Talk to him, Crassus </s>
<s> You know his speech" </s>
<s> The Roman officer turned to the giant </s>
<s> "Caesar says that you are to come with him, and he will make you the servant at his door" </s>
<s> The Barbarian rose, and his fair cheeks flushed with resentment </s>
<s> "I will serve Caesar as a soldier," said he, "but I will be house-servant to no man-not even to him </s>
<s> If Caesar would see what manner of man I am, let him put one of his guardsmen up against me" </s>
<s> "By the shade of Milo this is a bold fellow" </s>
<s> cried the Emperor </s>
<s> "How say you, Crassus </s>
<s> Shall he make good his words" </s>
<s> "By your leave, Caesar," said the blunt soldier, "good swordsmen are too rare in these days that we should let them slay each other for sport </s>
<s> Perhaps if the Barbarian would wrestle a fall--" "Excellent" </s>
<s> cried the Emperor </s>
<s> "Here is the Python, and here Varus the Lictor, each stripped for the bout </s>
<s> Have a look at them, Barbarian, and see which you would choose </s>
<s> What does he say </s>
<s> He would take them both </s>
<s> Nay then he is either the king of wrestlers or the king of boasters, and we shall soon see which </s>
<s> Let him have his way, and he has himself to thank if he comes out with a broken neck" </s>
<s> There was some laughter when the peasant tossed his sheep-skin mantle to the ground and, without troubling to remove his leathern tunic, advanced towards the two wrestlers; but it became uproarious when with a quick spring he seized the Greek under one arm and the Roman under the other, holding them as in a vice </s>
<s> Then with a terrific effort he tore them both from the ground, carried them writhing and kicking round the arena, and finally walking up to the Emperor's throne, threw his two athletes down in front of him </s>
<s> Then, bowing to Caesar, the huge Barbarian withdrew, and laid his great bulk down among the ranks of the applauding soldiers, whence he watched with stolid unconcern the conclusion of the sports </s>
<s> It was still daylight, when the last event had been decided, and the soldiers returned to the camp </s>
<s> The Emperor Severus had ordered his horse, and in the company of Crassus, his favourite prefect, rode down the winding pathway which skirts the Harpessus, chatting over the future dispersal of the army </s>
<s> They had ridden for some miles when Severus, glancing behind him, was surprised to see a huge figure which trotted lightly along at the very heels of his horse </s>
<s> "Surely this is Mercury as well as Hercules that we have found among the Thracian mountains," said he with a smile </s>
<s> "Let us see how soon our Syrian horses can out-distance him" </s>
<s> The two Romans broke into a gallop, and did not draw rein until a good mile had been covered at the full pace of their splendid chargers </s>
<s> Then they turned and looked back; but there, some distance off, still running with a lightness and a spring which spoke of iron muscles and inexhaustible endurance, came the great Barbarian </s>
<s> The Roman Emperor waited until the athlete had come up to them </s>
<s> "Why do you follow me" </s>
<s> he asked </s>
<s> "It is my hope, Caesar, that I may always follow you" </s>
<s> His flushed face as he spoke was almost level with that of the mounted Roman </s>
<s> "By the god of war, I do not know where in all the world I could find such a servant" </s>
<s> cried the Emperor </s>
<s> "You shall be my own body-guard, the one nearest to me of all" </s>
<s> The giant fell upon his knee </s>
<s> "My life and strength are yours," he said </s>
<s> "I ask no more than to spend them for Caesar" </s>
<s> Crassus had interpreted this short dialogue </s>
<s> He now turned to the Emperor </s>
<s> "If he is indeed to be always at your call, Caesar, it would be well to give the poor Barbarian some name which your lips can frame </s>
<s> Theckla is as uncouth and craggy a word as one of his native rocks" </s>
<s> The Emperor pondered for a moment </s>
<s> "If I am to have the naming of him," said he, "then surely I shall call him Maximus, for there is not such a giant upon earth" </s>
<s> "Hark you," said the Prefect </s>
<s> "The Emperor has deigned to give you a Roman name, since you have come into his service </s>
<s> Henceforth you are no longer Theckla, but you are Maximus </s>
<s> Can you say it after me" </s>
<s> "Maximin," repeated the Barbarian, trying to catch the Roman word </s>
<s> The Emperor laughed at the mincing accent </s>
<s> "Yes, yes, Maximin let it be </s>
<s> To all the world you are Maximin, the body-guard of Severus </s>
<s> When we have reached Rome, we will soon see that your dress shall correspond with your office </s>
<s> Meanwhile march with the guard until you have my further orders" </s>
<s> So it came about that as the Roman army resumed its march next day, and left behind it the fair valley of the Harpessus, a huge recruit, clad in brown leather, with a rude sheep-skin floating from his shoulders, marched beside the Imperial troop </s>
<s> But far away in the wooden farmhouse of a distant Macedonian valley two old country folk wept salt tears, and prayed to the gods for the safety of their boy who had turned his face to Rome </s>
<s> II THE RISE OF GIANT MAXIMIN Exactly twenty-five years had passed since the day that Theckla the huge Thracian peasant had turned into Maximin the Roman guardsman </s>
<s> They had not been good years for Rome </s>
<s> Gone for ever were the great Imperial days of the Hadrians and the Trajans </s>
<s> Gone also the golden age of the two Antonines, when the highest were for once the most worthy and most wise </s>
<s> It had been an epoch of weak and cruel men </s>
<s> Severus, the swarthy African, a stark grim man, had died in far away York, after fighting all the winter with the Caledonian Highlanders--a race who have ever since worn the martial garb of the Romans </s>
<s> His son, known only by his slighting nick-name of Caracalla, had reigned during six years of insane lust and cruelty, before the knife of an angry soldier avenged the dignity of the Roman name </s>
<s> The nonentity Macrinus had filled the dangerous throne for a single year before he also met a bloody end, and made room for the most grotesque of all monarchs, the unspeakable Heliogabalus with his foul mind and his painted face </s>
<s> He in turn was cut to pieces by the soldiers, and Severus Alexander, a gentle youth, scarce seventeen years of age, had been thrust into his place </s>
<s> For thirteen years now he had ruled, striving with some success to put some virtue and stability into the rotting Empire, but raising many fierce enemies as he did so-enemies whom he had not the strength nor the wit to hold in check </s>
<s> And Giant Maximin--what of him </s>
<s> He had carried his eight feet of manhood through the lowlands of Scotland, and the passes of the Grampians </s>
<s> He had seen Severus pass away, and had soldiered with his son </s>
<s> He had fought in Armenia, in Dacia, and in Germany </s>
<s> They had made him a centurion upon the field when with his hands he plucked out one by one the stockades of a northern village, and so cleared a path for the stormers </s>
<s> His strength had been the jest and the admiration of the soldiers </s>
<s> Legends about him had spread through the army and were the common gossip round the camp fires--of his duel with the German axeman on the Island of the Rhine, and of the blow with his fist which broke the leg of a Scythian's horse </s>
<s> Gradually he had won his way upwards, until now, after quarter of a century's service he was tribune of the fourth legion and superintendent of recruits for the whole army </s>
<s> The young soldier who had come under the glare of Maximin's eyes, or had been lifted up with one huge hand while he was cuffed by the other, had his first lesson from him in the discipline of the service </s>
<s> It was nightfall in the camp of the fourth legion upon the Gallic shore of the Rhine </s>
<s> Across the moonlit water, amid the thick forests which stretched away to the dim horizon, lay the wild untamed German tribes </s>
<s> Down on the river bank the light gleamed upon the helmets of the Roman sentinels who kept guard along the river </s>
<s> Far away a red point rose and fell in the darkness--a watch-fire of the enemy upon the further shore </s>
<s> Outside his tent, beside some smouldering logs, Giant Maximin was seated, a dozen of his officers around him </s>
<s> He had changed much since the day when we first met him in the Valley of the Harpessus </s>
<s> His huge frame was as erect as ever, and there was no sign of diminution of his strength </s>
<s> But he had aged none the less </s>
<s> The yellow tangle of hair was gone, worn down by the ever-pressing helmet </s>
<s> The fresh young face was drawn and hardened, with austere lines wrought by trouble and privation </s>
<s> The nose was more hawk-like, the eyes more cunning, the expression more cynical and more sinister </s>
<s> In his youth, a child would have run to his arms </s>
<s> Now it would shrink screaming from his gaze </s>
<s> That was what twenty-five years with the eagles had done for Theckla the Thracian peasant </s>
<s> He was listening now--for he was a man of few words--to the chatter of his centurions </s>
<s> One of them, Balbus the Sicilian, had been to the main camp at Mainz, only four miles away, and had seen the Emperor Alexander arrive that very day from Rome </s>
<s> The rest were eager at the news, for it was a time of unrest, and the rumour of great changes was in the air </s>
<s> "How many had he with him" </s>
<s> asked Labienus, a black-browed veteran from the south of Gaul </s>
<s> "I'll wager a month's pay that he was not so trustful as to come alone among his faithful legions" </s>
<s> "He had no great force," replied Balbus </s>
<s> "Ten or twelve cohorts of the Praetorians and a handful of horse" </s>
<s> "Then indeed his head is in the lion's mouth," cried Sulpicius, a hot-headed youth from the African Pentapolis </s>
<s> "How was he received" </s>
<s> "Coldly enough </s>
<s> There was scarce a shout as he came down the line" </s>
<s> "They are ripe for mischief," said Labienus </s>
<s> "And who can wonder, when it is we soldiers who uphold the Empire upon our spears, while the lazy citizens at Rome reap all of our sowing </s>
<s> Why cannot a soldier have what a soldier gains </s>
<s> So long as they throw us our denarius a day, they think that they have done with us" </s>
<s> "Aye," croaked a grumbling old greybeard </s>
<s> "Our limbs, our blood, our lives--what do they care so long as the Barbarians are held off, and they are left in peace to their feastings and their circus </s>
<s> Free bread, free wine, free games--everything for the loafer at Rome </s>
<s> For us the frontier guard and a soldier's fare" </s>
<s> Maximin gave a deep laugh </s>
<s> "Old Plancus talks like that," said he; "but we know that for all the world he would not change his steel plate for a citizen's gown </s>
<s> You've earned the kennel, old hound, if you wish it </s>
<s> Go and gnaw your bone and growl in peace" </s>
<s> "Nay, I am too old for change </s>
<s> I will follow the eagle till I die </s>
<s> And yet I had rather die in serving a soldier master than a long-gowned Syrian who comes of a stock where the women are men and the men are women" </s>
<s> There was a laugh from the circle of soldiers, for sedition and mutiny were rife in the camp, and even the old centurion's outbreak could not draw a protest </s>

<s> III THE FALL OF MAXIMIN For three years the soldier Emperor had been upon the throne </s>
<s> His palace had been his tent, and his people had been the legionaries </s>
<s> With them he was supreme; away from them he was nothing </s>
<s> He had gone with them from one frontier to the other </s>
<s> He had fought against Dacians, Sarmatians, and once again against the Germans </s>
<s> But Rome knew nothing of him, and all her turbulence rose against a master who cared so little for her or her opinion that he never deigned to set foot within her walls </s>
<s> There were cabals and conspiracies against the absent Caesar </s>
<s> Then his heavy hand fell upon them, and they were cuffed, even as the young soldiers had been who passed under his discipline </s>
<s> He knew nothing, and cared as much for consuls, senates, and civil laws </s>
<s> His own will and the power of the sword were the only forces which he could understand </s>
<s> Of commerce and the arts he was as ignorant as when he left his Thracian home </s>
<s> The whole vast Empire was to him a huge machine for producing the money by which the legions were to be rewarded </s>
<s> Should he fail to get that money, his fellow soldiers would bear him a grudge </s>
<s> To watch their interests they had raised him upon their shields that night </s>
<s> If city funds had to be plundered or temples desecrated, still the money must be got </s>

<s> But there came resistance, and all the fierce energy of the man, all the hardness which had given him the leadership of hard men, sprang forth to quell it </s>

<s> Life and death were cheap things to him </s>
<s> He struck savagely at all who stood up to him, and when they hit back, he struck more savagely still </s>

<s> He sat by the hour with his craggy chin between his hands, and his elbows resting on his knees, while he recalled all the misadventures, all the vexations of his early youth, when Roman wits had shot their little satires upon his bulk and his ignorance </s>
<s> He could not write, but his son Verus placed the names upon his tablets, and they were sent to the Governor of Rome </s>
<s> Men who had long forgotten their offence were called suddenly to make most bloody reparation </s>
<s> A rebellion broke out in Africa, but was quelled by his lieutenant </s>
<s> But the mere rumour of it set Rome in a turmoil </s>
<s> The Senate found something of its ancient spirit </s>
<s> So did the Italian people </s>
<s> They would not be for ever bullied by the legions </s>
<s> As Maximin approached from the frontier, with the sack of rebellious Rome in his mind, he was faced with every sign of a national resistance </s>
<s> The countryside was deserted, the farms abandoned, the fields cleared of crops and cattle </s>

<s> Against you they have no quarrel </s>
<s> Why should they mishandle you </s>
<s> Keep far from Rome and the Romans </s>
<s> Old Eudoxus has money, and to spare </s>
<s> He awaits you with two horses outside the camp </s>
<s> Make for the valley of the Harpessus, lad </s>
<s> It was thence that your father came, and there you will find his kin </s>
<s> Buy and stock a homestead, and keep yourself far from the paths of greatness and of danger </s>

<s> When his son had kissed his hand and had left him, the Emperor drew his robe around him and sat long in thought </s>

<s> they cried </s>
<s> "The tyrant is dead," and from all the camp beneath them and from the walls of the beleaguered city the joyous cry came echoing back, "He is dead, Maximin is dead" </s>
<s> I sit in my study, and upon the table before me lies a denarius of Maximin, as fresh as when the triumvir of the Temple of Juno Moneta sent it from the mint </s>
<s> Around it are recorded his resounding titles--Imperator Maximinus, Pontifex Maximus, Tribunitia potestate, and the rest </s>

<s> For all the pompous roll of titles it is a peasant's face, and I see him not as the Emperor of Rome, but as the great Thracian boor who strode down the hillside on that far-distant summer day when first the eagles beckoned him to Rome </s>
<s> THE COMING OF THE HUNS In the middle of the fourth century the state of the Christian religion was a scandal and a disgrace </s>
<s> Patient, humble, and long-suffering in adversity, it had become positive, aggressive, and unreasonable with success </s>
<s> Paganism was not yet dead, but it was rapidly sinking, finding its most faithful supporters among the conservative aristocrats of the best families on the one hand, and among those benighted villagers on the other who gave their name to the expiring creed </s>
<s> Between these two extremes the great majority of reasonable men had turned from the conception of many gods to that of one, and had rejected for ever the beliefs of their forefathers </s>
<s> But with the vices of polytheism they had also abandoned its virtues, among which toleration and religious good humour had been conspicuous </s>
<s> The strenuous earnestness of the Christians had compelled them to examine and define every point of their own theology; but as they had no central authority by which such definitions could be checked, it was not long before a hundred heresies had put forward their rival views, while the same earnestness of conviction led the stronger bands of schismatics to endeavour, for conscience sake, to force their views upon the weaker, and thus to cover the Eastern world with confusion and strife </s>
<s> Alexandria, Antioch, and Constantinople were centres of theological warfare </s>
<s> The whole north of Africa, too, was rent by the strife of the Donatists, who upheld their particular schism by iron flails and the war-cry of "Praise to the Lord" </s>
<s> But minor local controversies sank to nothing when compared with the huge argument of the Catholic and the Arian, which rent every village in twain, and divided every household from the cottage to the palace </s>
<s> The rival doctrines of the Homoousian and of the Homoiousian, containing metaphysical differences so attenuated that they could hardly be stated, turned bishop against bishop and congregation against congregation </s>
<s> The ink of the theologians and the blood of the fanatics were spilled in floods on either side, and gentle followers of Christ were horrified to find that their faith was responsible for such a state of riot and bloodshed as had never yet disgraced the religious history of the world </s>
<s> Many of the more earnest among them, shocked and scandalized, slipped away to the Libyan Desert, or to the solitude of Pontus, there to await in self-denial and prayer that second coming which was supposed to be at hand </s>
<s> Even in the deserts they could not escape the echo of the distant strife, and the hermits themselves scowled fiercely from their dens at passing travellers who might be contaminated by the doctrines of Athanasius or of Arius </s>
<s> Such a hermit was Simon Melas, of whom I write </s>
<s> A Trinitarian and a Catholic, he was shocked by the excesses of the persecution of the Arians, which could be only matched by the similar outrages with which these same Arians in the day of their power avenged their treatment on their brother Christians </s>
<s> Weary of the whole strife, and convinced that the end of the world was indeed at hand, he left his home in Constantinople and travelled as far as the Gothic settlements in Dacia, beyond the Danube, in search of some spot where he might be free from the never-ending disputes </s>
<s> Still journeying to the north and east, he crossed the river which we now call the Dneister, and there, finding a rocky hill rising from an immense plain, he formed a cell near its summit, and settled himself down to end his life in self-denial and meditation </s>
<s> There were fish in the stream, the country teemed with game, and there was an abundance of wild fruits, so that his spiritual exercises were not unduly interrupted by the search of sustenance for his mortal frame </s>
<s> In this distant retreat he expected to find absolute solitude, but the hope was in vain </s>
<s> Within a week of his arrival, in an hour of worldly curiosity, he explored the edges of the high rocky hill upon which he lived </s>
<s> Making his way up to a cleft, which was hung with olives and myrtles, he came upon a cave in the opening of which sat an aged man, white-bearded, white-haired, and infirm--a hermit like himself </s>
<s> So long had this stranger been alone that he had almost forgotten the use of his tongue; but at last, words coming more freely, he was able to convey the information that his name was Paul of Nicopolis, that he was a Greek citizen, and that he also had come out into the desert for the saving of his soul, and to escape from the contamination of heresy </s>
<s> "Little I thought, brother Simon," said he, "that I should ever find any one else who had come so far upon the same holy errand </s>
<s> In all these years, and they are so many that I have lost count of them, I have never seen a man, save indeed one or two wandering shepherds far out upon yonder plain" </s>
<s> From where they sat, the huge steppe, covered with waving grass and gleaming with a vivid green in the sun, stretched away as level and as unbroken as the sea, to the eastern horizon </s>
<s> Simon Melas stared across it with curiosity </s>
<s> "Tell me, brother Paul," said he, "you who have lived here so long--what lies at the further side of that plain" </s>
<s> The old man shook his head </s>
<s> "There is no further side to the plain," said he </s>
<s> "It is the earth's boundary, and stretches away to eternity </s>
<s> For all these years I have sat beside it, but never once have I seen anything come across it </s>
<s> It is manifest that if there had been a further side there would certainly at some time have come some traveller from that direction </s>
<s> Over the great river yonder is the Roman post of Tyras; but that is a long day's journey from here, and they have never disturbed my meditations" </s>
<s> "On what do you meditate, brother Paul" </s>
<s> "At first I meditated on many sacred mysteries; but now, for twenty years, I have brooded continually on the nature of the Logos </s>
<s> What is your view upon that vital matter, brother Simon" </s>
<s> "Surely," said the younger man, "there can be no question as to that </s>
<s> The Logos is assuredly but a name used by St </s>
<s> John to signify the Deity" </s>
<s> The old hermit gave a hoarse cry of fury, and his brown, withered face was convulsed with anger </s>
<s> Seizing the huge cudgel which he kept to beat off the wolves, he shook it murderously at his companion </s>
<s> "Out with you </s>
<s> Out of my cell" </s>
<s> he cried </s>
<s> "Have I lived here so long to have it polluted by a vile Trinitarian--a follower of the rascal Athanasius </s>
<s> Wretched idolater, learn once for all, that the Logos is in truth an emanation from the Deity, and in no sense equal or co-eternal with Him </s>
<s> Out with you, I say, or I will dash out your brains with my staff" </s>
<s> It was useless to reason with the furious Arian, and Simon withdrew in sadness and wonder, that at this extreme verge of the known earth the spirit of religious strife should still break upon the peaceful solitude of the wilderness </s>
<s> With hanging head and heavy heart he made his way down the valley, and climbed up once more to his own cell, which lay at the crown of the hill, with the intention of never again exchanging visits with his Arian neighbour </s>
<s> Here, for a year, dwelt Simon Melas, leading a life of solitude and prayer </s>
<s> There was no reason why any one should ever come to this outermost point of human habitation </s>
<s> Once a young Roman officer--Caius Crassus--rode out a day's journey from Tyras, and climbed the hill to have speech with the anchorite </s>
<s> He was of an equestrian family, and still held his belief in the old dispensation </s>
<s> He looked with interest and surprise, but also with some disgust, at the ascetic arrangements of that humble abode </s>
<s> "Whom do you please by living in such a fashion" </s>
<s> he asked </s>
<s> "We show that our spirit is superior to our flesh," Simon answered </s>
<s> "If we fare badly in this world, we believe that we shall reap an advantage in the world to come" </s>
<s> The centurion shrugged his shoulders </s>
<s> "There are philosophers among our people, Stoics and others, who have the same idea </s>
<s> When I was in the Herulian Cohort of the Fourth Legion we were quartered in Rome itself, and I saw much of the Christians, but I could never learn anything from them which I had not heard from my own father, whom you, in your arrogance, would call a Pagan </s>
<s> It is true that we talk of numerous gods; but for many years we have not taken them very seriously </s>
<s> Our thoughts upon virtue and duty and a noble life are the same as your own" </s>
<s> Simon Melas shook his head </s>
<s> "If you have not the holy books," said he, "then what guide have you to direct your steps" </s>
<s> "If you will read our philosophers, and above all the divine Plato, you will find that there are other guides who may take you to the same end </s>
<s> Have you by chance read the book which was written by our Emperor Marcus Aurelius </s>
<s> Do you not discover there every virtue which man could have, although he knew nothing of your creed </s>
<s> Have you considered, also, the words and actions of our late Emperor Julian, with whom I served my first campaign when he went out against the Persians </s>
<s> Where could you find a more perfect man than he" </s>
<s> "Such talk is unprofitable, and I will have no more of it," said Simon, sternly </s>
<s> "Take heed while there is time, and embrace the true faith; for the end of the world is at hand, and when it comes there will be no mercy for those who have shut their eyes to the light" </s>
<s> So saying, he turned back once more to his praying-stool and to his crucifix, while the young Roman walked in deep thought down the hill, and mounting his horse, rode off to his distant post </s>
<s> Simon watched him until his brazen helmet was but a bead of light on the western edge of the great plain; for this was the first human face that he had seen in all this long year, and there were times when his heart yearned for the voices and the faces of his kind </s>
<s> So another year passed, and save for the chance of weather and the slow change of the seasons, one day was as another </s>
<s> Every morning, when Simon opened his eyes, he saw the same grey line ripening into red in the furthest east, until the bright rim pushed itself above that far-off horizon across which no living creature had ever been known to come </s>
<s> Slowly the sun swept across the huge arch of the heavens, and as the shadows shifted from the black rocks which jutted upward from above his cell, so did the hermit regulate his terms of prayer and meditation </s>
<s> There was nothing on earth to draw his eye, or to distract his mind, for the grassy plain below was as void from month to month as the heaven above </s>
<s> So the long hours passed, until the red rim slipped down on the further side, and the day ended in the same pearl-grey shimmer with which it had begun </s>
<s> Once two ravens circled for some days round the lonely hill, and once a white fish-eagle came from the Dneister and screamed above the hermit's head </s>
<s> Sometimes red dots were seen on the green plain where the antelopes grazed, and often a wolf howled in the darkness from the base of the rocks </s>
<s> Such was the uneventful life of Simon Melas the anchorite, until there came the day of wrath </s>
<s> It was in the late spring of the year 375 that Simon came out from his cell, his gourd in his hand, to draw water from the spring </s>
<s> Darkness had closed in, the sun had set, but one last glimmer of rosy light rested upon a rocky peak, which jutted forth from the hill, on the further side from the hermit's dwelling </s>
<s> As Simon came forth from under his ledge, the gourd dropped from his hand, and he stood gazing in amazement </s>
<s> On the opposite peak a man was standing, his outline black in the fading light </s>
<s> He was a strange almost a deformed figure, short-statured, round-backed, with a large head, no neck, and a long rod jutting out from between his shoulders </s>
<s> He stood with his face advanced, and his body bent, peering very intently over the plain to the westward </s>
<s> In a moment he was gone, and the lonely black peak showed up hard and naked against the faint eastern glimmer </s>
<s> Then the night closed down, and all was black once more </s>
<s> Simon Melas stood long in bewilderment, wondering who this stranger could be </s>
<s> He had heard, as had every Christian, of those evil spirits which were wont to haunt the hermits in the Thebaid and on the skirts of the Ethiopian waste </s>
<s> The strange shape of this solitary creature, its dark outline and prowling, intent attitude, suggestive rather of a fierce, rapacious beast than of a man, all helped him to believe that he had at last encountered one of those wanderers from the pit, of whose existence, in those days of robust faith, he had no more doubt than of his own </s>
<s> Much of the night he spent in prayer, his eyes glancing continually at the low arch of his cell door, with its curtain of deep purple wrought with stars </s>
<s> At any instant some crouching monster, some homed abomination, might peer in upon him; and he clung with frenzied appeal to his crucifix, as his human weakness quailed at the thought </s>
<s> But at last his fatigue overcame his fears, and falling upon his couch of dried grass, he slept until the bright daylight brought him to his senses </s>
<s> It was later than was his wont, and the sun was far above the horizon </s>
<s> As he came forth from his cell, he looked across at the peak of rock, but it stood there bare and silent </s>
<s> Already it seemed to him that that strange dark figure which had startled him so was some dream, some vision of the twilight </s>
<s> His gourd lay where it had fallen, and he picked it up with the intention of going to the spring </s>
<s> But suddenly he was aware of something new </s>
<s> The whole air was throbbing with sound </s>
<s> From all sides it came, rumbling, indefinite, an inarticulate mutter, low, but thick and strong, rising, falling, reverberating among the rocks, dying away into vague whispers, but always there </s>
<s> He looked round at the blue, cloudless sky in bewilderment </s>
<s> Then he scrambled up the rocky pinnacle above him, and sheltering himself in its shadow, he stared out over the plain </s>
<s> In his wildest dream he had never imagined such a sight </s>
<s> The whole vast expanse was covered with horse-men, hundreds and thousands and tens of thousands, all riding slowly and in silence, out of the unknown east </s>
<s> It was the multitudinous beat of their horses' hoofs which caused that low throbbing in his ears </s>
<s> Some were so close to him as he looked down upon them that he could see clearly their thin wiry horses, and the strange humped figures of the swarthy riders, sitting forward on the withers, shapeless bundles, their short legs hanging stirrupless, their bodies balanced as firmly as though they were part of the beast </s>
<s> In those nearest he could see the bow and the quiver, the long spear and the short sword, with the coiled lasso behind the rider, which told that this was no helpless horde of wanderers, but a formidable army upon the march </s>
<s> His eyes passed on from them and swept further and further, but still to the very horizon, which quivered with movement, there was no end to this monstrous cavalry </s>
<s> Already the vanguard was far past the island of rock upon which he dwelt, and he could now understand that in front of this vanguard were single scouts who guided the course of the army, and that it was one of these whom he had seen the evening before </s>
<s> All day, held spell-bound by this wonderful sight, the hermit crouched in the shadow of the rocks, and all day the sea of horsemen rolled onward over the plain beneath </s>
<s> Simon had seen the swarming quays of Alexandria, he had watched the mob which blocked the hippodrome of Constantinople, yet never had he imagined such a multitude as now defiled beneath his eyes, coming from that eastern skyline which had been the end of his world </s>
<s> Sometimes the dense streams of horsemen were broken by droves of brood-mares and foals, driven along by mounted guards; sometimes there were herds of cattle; sometimes there were lines of waggons with skin canopies above them; but then once more, after every break, came the horsemen, the horsemen, the hundreds and the thousands and the tens of thousands, slowly, ceaselessly, silently drifting from the east to the west </s>
<s> The long day passed, the light waned, and the shadows fell; but still the great broad stream was flowing by </s>

<s> History told him how the Roman world had ever been assailed by fresh swarms of Barbarians, coming from the outer darkness, and that the Eastern Empire had already, in its fifty years of existence since Constantine had moved the capital of the world to the shores of the Bosphorus, been tormented in the same way </s>

<s> THE FIRST CARGO "Ex ovo omnia" When you left Briton with your legion, my dear Crassus, I promised that I would write to you from time to time when a messenger chanced to be going to Rome, and keep you informed as to anything of interest which might occur in this country </s>
<s> Personally, I am very glad that I remained behind when the troops and so many of our citizens left, for though the living is rough and the climate is infernal, still by dint of the three voyages which I have made for amber to the Baltic, and the excellent prices which I obtained for it here, I shall soon be in a position to retire, and to spend my old age under my own fig tree, or even perhaps to buy a small villa at Baiae or Posuoli, where I could get a good sun-bath after the continued fogs of this accursed island </s>
<s> I picture myself on a little farm, and I read the Georgics as a preparation; but when I hear the rain falling and the wind howling, Italy seems very far away </s>
<s> In my previous letter, I let you know how things were going in this country </s>
<s> The poor folk, who had given up all soldiering during the centuries that we guarded them, are now perfectly helpless before these Picts and Scots, tattoed Barbarians from the north, who overrun the whole country and do exactly what they please </s>
<s> So long as they kept to the north, the people in the south, who are the most numerous, and also the most civilized of the Britons, took no heed of them; but now the rascals have come as far as London, and the lazy folk in these parts have had to wake up </s>
<s> Vortigern, the king, is useless for anything but drink or women, so he sent across to the Baltic to get over some of the North Germans, in the hope that they would come and help him </s>
<s> It is bad enough to have a bear in your house, but it does not seem to me to mend matters if you call in a pack of ferocious wolves as well </s>
<s> However, nothing better could be devised, so an invitation was sent and very promptly accepted </s>
<s> And it is here that your humble friend appears upon the scene </s>
<s> In the course of my amber trading I had learned the Saxon speech, and so I was sent down in all haste to the Kentish shore that I might be there when our new allies came </s>
<s> I arrived there on the very day when their first vessel appeared, and it is of my adventures that I wish to tell you </s>
<s> It is perfectly clear to me that the landing of these warlike Germans in England will prove to be an event of historical importance, and so your inquisitive mind will not feel wearied if I treat the matter in some detail </s>
<s> It was, then, upon the day of Mercury, immediately following the Feast of Our Blessed Lord's Ascension, that I found myself upon the south bank of the river Thames, at the point where it opens into a wide estuary </s>
<s> There is an island there named Thanet, which was the spot chosen for the landfall of our visitors </s>
<s> Sure enough, I had no sooner ridden up than there was a great red ship, the first as it seems of three, coming in under full sail </s>
<s> The white horse, which is the ensign of these rovers, was hanging from her topmast, and she appeared to be crowded with men </s>
<s> The sun was shining brightly, and the great scarlet ship, with snow-white sails and a line of gleaming shields slung over her side, made as fair a picture on that blue expanse as one would wish to see </s>
<s> I pushed off at once in a boat, because it had been arranged that none of the Saxons should land until the king had come down to speak with their leaders </s>
<s> Presently I was under the ship, which had a gilded dragon in the bows, and a tier of oars along either side </s>
<s> As I looked up, there was a row of helmeted heads looking down at me, and among them I saw, to my great surprise and pleasure, that of Eric the Swart, with whom I do business at Venta every year </s>
<s> He greeted me heartily when I reached the deck, and became at once my guide, friend, and counsellor </s>
<s> This helped me greatly with these Barbarians, for it is their nature that they are very cold and aloof unless one of their own number can vouch for you, after which they are very hearty and hospitable </s>
<s> Try as they will, they find it hard, however, to avoid a certain suggestion of condescension, and in the baser sort, of contempt, when they are dealing with a foreigner </s>
<s> It was a great stroke of luck meeting Eric, for he was able to give me some idea of how things stood before I was shown into the presence of Kenna, the leader of this particular ship </s>
<s> The crew, as I learned from him, was entirely made up of three tribes or families--those of Kenna, of Lanc, and of Hasta </s>
<s> Each of these tribes gets its name by putting the letters "ing" after the name of the chief, so that the people on board would describe themselves as Kennings, Lancings, and Hastings </s>
<s> I observed in the Baltic that the villages were named after the family who lived in them, each keeping to itself, so that I have no doubt if these fellows get a footing on shore, we shall see settlements with names like these rising up among the British towns </s>
<s> The greater part of the men were sturdy fellows with red, yellow, or brown hair, mostly the latter </s>
<s> To my surprise, I saw several women among them </s>
<s> Eric, in answer to my question, explained that they always take their women with them so far as they can, and that instead of finding them an incumbrance as our Roman dames would be, they look upon them as helpmates and advisers </s>
<s> Of course, I remembered afterwards that our excellent and accurate Tacitus has remarked upon this characteristic of the Germans </s>
<s> All laws in the tribes are decided by votes, and a vote has not yet been given to the women, but many are in favour of it, and it is thought that woman and man may soon have the same power in the State, though many of the women themselves are opposed to such an innovation </s>
<s> I observed to Eric that it was fortunate there were several women on board, as they could keep each other company; but he answered that the wives of chiefs had no desire to know the wives of the inferior officers, and that both of them combined against the more common women, so that any companionship was out of the question </s>
<s> He pointed as he spoke to Editha, the wife of Kenna, a red-faced, elderly woman, who walked among the others, her chin in the air, taking no more notice than if they did not exist </s>
